<h2><a name="_Toc25595333"></a><a name="_Toc20910678"></a><a name="_Toc20852657"></a><a

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=RU style='mso-ansi-language:RU'><br>
</span><span lang=RU style='font-size:14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;

&#1089;&#1086;&#1073;&#1086;&#1081; &#1073;&#1072;&#1079;&#1091;
&#1076;&#1072;&#1085;&#1085;&#1099;&#1093; </span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>MS</span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;

10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>SQL</span><span style='font-size:
14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-ansi-language:RU'> </span><span style='font-size:14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:

mso-ansi-language:RU'> 2018,
&#1074;&#1077;&#1073;-&#1089;&#1077;&#1088;&#1074;&#1077;&#1088; </span><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>IIS</span><span

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span

  <td width=518 style='width:310.95pt;border:solid #999999 1.0pt;border-left:

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-layout-grid-align:
  none;text-autospace:none'><span lang=RU style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:
